 ) The Supreme Court has made a big comment related to women's rights
 court ne ek cese kii sunwaayee ke dauraan kaha he ki pati apni patni ko jabardastee saath rahane ke liye nahin kah saktaa he
 Actually, the husband was accused of cruelty on behalf of a woman
 isse jude cese kii sunwaayee ke dauraan supreme court ne yah tippanee kii
 The woman said in her charge that the husband wants her to live with him but she does not want to be with her husband
 mahila ke is dard ko dhyaan main rakhte hue supreme court ne pati ke khilaaf sakht tippanee kii
 The court said that the wife is not a 'movable property' or 'thing'
 isliye patni ke saath rahane kii ichha hone ke baavjood pati iske liye patni par dawaab nahin bana saktaa he
 What the court said: The bench of Justices Madan B
 Lokur and Deepak Gupta told the husband of the woman present in the court, 'she is not a movable property

 Some of the standards set by a committee of external experts may soon assess the country's central universities
 maanav sansaadhan vikaas mantralay bhartiya praudyogiki sansthaanon (iaiti) main paalan kiye jane vaale niyamon kii tarj par kendriya vishvavidhyalayon ke liye ek bahari pear samiksha (eepiaar) tantra sthapit karne par vichaar kar rahaa he
 In a recent meeting, sources said, HRD Minister Smriti Irani asked her officials to consider the possibility of introducing an external peer review (EPR) mechanism to assess central universities on the lines of iits
 ek aadhikarik sutara ne bataaya, ‘‘bahari pear samiksha ek aisa tantra he jiske tahat shikshan, shodh evam udyog ke visheshgyon kii ek samiti har paanch saal par kuch tay maanakon par kisi iaiti ke pradarshan kaa akalan karte hai
 Following the minister's suggestion, the ministry is considering the possibility of introducing this system for central universities as well
 ’’ tippaniyan There are more than 40 central universities in the country and it is possible that teams of officials of one university review the other based on the format decided
 baharhaal, aisi samiksha ke swaroop ko antim rup dene ke liye jaruri kadam uthaae jaaenge
 Sources said the University Grants Commission (UGC) may also be involved in finalizing the details of the peer review process for universities
 sutron ne bataaya ki ek haalia baithak main maanav sansaadhan vikaas mantri smriti irani ne apane adhikariyon se kaha ki ve iaiti kii tarj par kendriya vishvavidhyalayon ke akalan ke liye bhi bahari pear samiksha (eepiaar) tantra shuru karne kii sambhaavna par vichaar karen
 "an external peer review is a mechanism under which a committee of experts from teaching, research and industry assess the performance of an IIT on certain set standards every five years," an official source said
 mantri ke suzav ke baad mantralay is vyavastha ko kendriya vishvavidhyalayon ke liye bhi shuru karne kii sambhaavna par vichaar kar rahaa he 
 '' Comments desh main 40 se zyada kendriya vishvavidhyalay hai or sambhav he ki kisi ek vishvavidhyalay ke adhikariyon kii team tay kiye gaye swaroop ke aadhaar par anya kii samiksha kare
 However, necessary steps will be taken to finalize the nature of such a review
 sutron ne bataaya ki vishvavidhyalay anudaan ayog (ujisi) ko bhi vishvavidhyalayon ke liye pear samiksha prakriya ke byore ko antim rup dene ke kaam main shaamil kiya ja saktaa he

 Some of the measures to remove dark circles under men's eyes are as follows: Cucumber: The best way to treat dark circles is to use cucumber
 khiraa ek acha astrogent hota he or yah behtareen cleennjar bhi hota he jo ankhon ke neeche hone vaale kaale gheron ko khatm kar detaa he

 Sleep: Due to lack of proper sleep for a long time, dark circles under the eyes also occur

 When you take complete rest and relax the eyes, the dark circles will automatically be corrected

 (input from agency) silk kii saadiyaan aam saadiyon kii tulana main kuch mahangi hoti hai
 Apart from being expensive, silk saris also require proper maintenance
 sahi tareeke se nahin rakhane par silk kii saadiyaan kharaab ho jaati hai
 According to experts, the saris of Tosilk should be changed from time to time to keep them fresh for a long time
 unhen sooti yaa malamal ke kapade main lapetakar rakhana chahie
 These two measures are usually adopted in the homes of all of us, but if you believe Udayan Singh, the founder of the Banka Silk of Bihar, with the help of these measures, you can keep the silk like new for a long time
 - sooti kapade main lapetakar rakhen:apni silk kii saadiyon ko nayaa banaae rakhane ke liye unhen hameshaa sooti kapade main lapet kar rakhen
 Do not hang them in metal hangers and keep each saree under separate cover
 - dhoop dikhaaen:kuch-kuch dinon ke antaraal par inhen kapade se baahar nikaalkar dhoop dikhaaen
 This will keep their shine
 - tah badalen:saadiyon kii tahon ko badalte rahen
 Do not hang heavy saris in the cupboard
 - neem kii pattiyaan daalen:silk kii saadiyon cokide-makodon se bachaane ke lienim kii pattiyon kaa istemaal karen
 It is also good to use naphthalene tablets
 jab bhi aap inhen pahanen, inhen almaari main rakhane se pehle hawa main sukhaaen, taaki inamen kisi prakaar kii badboo na rah jaae
 Dry cleaning is the safest method for silk cleaning

 ’’ america main bharat kii rajdoot nirupama raav ne visconcin ke ok creek gurudware main hui golibari ke peedit pariwaron se mulaakaat kar puri madad kaa bharosa diya

 Cook has lived in two separate apartments in South Miliwaki with Page
 sangheey agenciyon ko abhi tak is bare main koi jaankaree nahin he ki aakhir purv sainik pej ne yah golibari kyon kii or iske pichhi uski manshaa kya thi
 Page was killed by police after the shootout

 philhal, hamalavar ke ghar, parivaar, doston, vyaktigat aankade, uske puraane aapraadhik record aadi ke bare main pataa kiya ja rahaa he
 It is noteworthy that the FBI is investigating this entire case but has made very little information public
 agency apni is jaanch ke dauraan nasli ghrinaa ke pahalu ke bare main bhi tahakikat kar rahi he

 milwauki gurudware main golibari kii ghatana ke baad police ne 41 varshiya purv sainik vade maaikel ko maar giraaya tha

 ‘sienen’ ke mutabik ok creek ke police pramukh jon edwards kaa kahana he, ‘‘ant main shaayad hamaare paas is bare main bahut saare tathy hon ki vah kin chizon se judaa hua tha, vah kiske saath judaa hua tha, lekin shaayad ham uski manshaa ke bare main kabhi jaan nahin sakenge, kyonki vah mar gaya he, or manshaa bhi uske saath hi mar gai he
 '' jaanchakarta vibhinn rajyon main isse jude taron ko khangaal rahe hai lekin media main aayi khabaron ke anusaar kanoon visheshgyon kaa maananaa he ki unhen in tathyon ko adaalat main pesh karne kaa mauka nahin milegaa

 yahaan khaas baat yah he ki america ke visconcin sthit gurudware main golibari karne vaala vade maaikel pej yahaan ke sangheey jaanch beuro (epabiai) ke radar par bilkul nahin tha
